[[overloaded-bf16-mode-switch-vector-widening-floating-point-add-subtract]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Widening Floating-Point Add/Subtract Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]
----
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwadd_vf(vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwadd_wv(vfloat32mf2_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwadd_wf(vfloat32mf2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1,
                               size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwadd_vf(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwadd_wv(vfloat32m1_t vs2, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwadd_wf(vfloat32m1_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwadd_vf(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwadd_wv(vfloat32m2_t vs2, vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwadd_wf(vfloat32m2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m4_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv(vbfloat16m2_t vs2, vbfloat16m2_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m4_t __riscv_vfwadd_vf(vbfloat16m2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m4_t __riscv_vfwadd_wv(vfloat32m4_t vs2, vbfloat16m2_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m4_t __riscv_vfwadd_wf(vfloat32m4_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m8_t __riscv_vfwadd_vv(vbfloat16m4_t vs2, vbfloat16m4_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m8_t __riscv_vfwadd_vf(vbfloat16m4_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m8_t __riscv_vfwadd_wv(vfloat32m8_t vs2, vbfloat16m4_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m8_t __riscv_vfwadd_wf(vfloat32m8_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);

                                size_t vl);

vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwsub_wv(vfloat32mf2_t vs2, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwsub_wf(vfloat32mf2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwsub_vv(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1,
                               size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwsub_vf(vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwsub_wv(vfloat32m1_t vs2, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwsub_wf(vfloat32m1_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwsub_vv(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwsub_vf(vbfloat16m1_t vs2, __bf16 rs1, size_t vl);
vfloat32m2_t __riscv_vfwsub_wv(vfloat32m2_t vs2, vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);

                              vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, size_t vl);

                             vbfloat16m1_t vs2, size_t vl);

                             size_t vl);

                             vbfloat16m2_t vs2, size_t vl);

                             size_t vl);

                             vbfloat16m4_t vs2, size_t vl);

[[overloaded-bf16-mode-switch-vector-widening-floating-point-fused-multiply-add]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Widening Floating-Point Fused Multiply-Add Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]
----
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwmacc(vfloat32mf2_t vd, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                              vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwmacc(vfloat32mf2_t vd, __bf16 vs1, vbfloat16mf4_t vs2,
                              size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwmacc(vfloat32m1_t vd, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1,
                             vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, size_t vl);

                             size_t vl);
